name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Themed Room
info:Stayed in May 2024

info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 6, 2024
msg:Having stayed at Jinling Hotel in Nanjing and Chongqing, I chose to stay at Jinling Hotel in Yangzhou this time. I was very satisfied with the service throughout the trip. Yangzhou is not big, and it is very convenient to call a taxi. You don't have to stay near the scenic spot. If you want to eat, you can dine in the hotel or the Fuchun Restaurant next to it, or take a taxi to the Colorful World store in Quyuan for a few minutes. The children's theme suite is suitable for bringing the elderly and children at the same time. It is much more convenient than booking two rooms, especially when the hotel rooms are tight. You don't have to consider taking the risk of two rooms being far away or even on different floors. That would be too troublesome. The suite has two bathrooms, which are enough for 4 people. Fruits and snacks are welcome, and yogurt is great. The hotel breakfast is also good, and the service staff is also very humane. In short, it was a very good stay experience.

msg:Front desk: This team has the best service, especially attentive and on-site. When we ordered takeaways, the robot was too busy to deliver them to the floor. Several lobby managers were always in the lobby to serve guests.
Restaurant: The breakfast variety is quite rich, the dishes are added in time, and the taste is good. What is particularly good is that there are dishes in every basin even when breakfast is open until 10:00, which is very good. However, some waiters' work clothes are too dirty.
Hardware: It is a little old and the decoration is old.
Surroundings: The location is a bit remote, and the square downstairs is dirty and messy.
Room: It was converted from the original suite. There is a large gap between the rooms, and you can clearly see the next room. The bedside sockets in the living room are very inconvenient. You must pull the bedside table open to use the bedside sockets. There are no windows in the two bathrooms, and there is a sewer smell. In addition, the air conditioning in the living room is not good. I told the front desk but it didn't improve. The room is very stuffy and has a strange smell. I have to open the window for ventilation.
Service: There are several lobby managers at the front desk who are very good. The security guard at the door also helps to open the car door and carry the luggage. The service of the guest room restaurant waiter is also very good. The service of the entire hotel is worthy of praise. The room price has increased slightly during holidays, and the hardware is slightly worse.

Jinling Hotel is a well-established five-star hotel, and it really lives up to its reputation. The service is very meticulous, the hygiene is very clean, and the buffet breakfast in the restaurant is very rich. There are fruit plates, homemade yogurt, and mineral water every day.
